<script type="text/javascript">
function updateSuccess(msg) {
    $(function() {
        if (msg) {
            toastr["success"](msg);
        } else {
            toastr["success"]('global.success');
        }
    })
}
function updateError(msg) {
    $(function() {
        if (msg) {
            toastr["error"](msg);
        } else {
            toastr["error"]('global.error');
        }
    })
}
function warningMessage(msg) {
    $(function() {
        toastr["warning"](msg);
    })
}
function processReturnMessage(returnCode, msg, callback, extraValue) {
    try {
        if (returnCode == 0 && msg != '') {
            if (msg) {
                updateSuccess(msg);
            } else {
                updateSuccess();
            }
        } else if (returnCode == 1 && msg != '') {
            if (msg) {
                updateError(msg);
            } else {
                updateError();
            }
        } else if (returnCode == 2 && msg != '') {
            if (msg) {
                warningMessage(msg);
            }
        }
        if (callback != null && callback != '') {
            setTimeout(function() {
                eval(callback + '(returnCode,extraValue,msg)');
            }, 50)
        }
    } catch (ex) {
        alert(ex.message);
    }
}
function scrollTop() {
    $("html, body").animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 400);
}
$(document).ready(function(){
    /*style and control input file*/
    $("html").on("keyup", ".file-control", function(e){
       var code = e.which;
       if(code == 13) {
           return $(this).find('input[type="file"]').trigger('click');;
       }
    });
    $("html").on("change", ".file-control > input[type='file']", function(e) {
         var $this = $(this);
         if (this.files && this.files[0]) {
            $this.parents('.file-control').addClass('hasFile').find('.file-text').html(this.files[0].name);
            $(this).prop('title',this.files[0].name);
            $this.parents('.file-control').addClass('hasFile').find('.btn-delete-file').attr("title", 'Xóa file');
         } else {
            $this.parents('.file-control').removeClass('hasFile').find('.file-text').html('Chưa có file được chọn');
            $(this).prop('title','Chưa có file được chọn');
         }
    })
    $("html").on("click", ".file-control > .btn-delete-file", function(e) {
         return $(this).parents('.file-control').find('input[type="file"]').val(null).trigger('change');
    })
    $.fn.inputFileControl = function() {
        return $(this).width('auto').wrap($('<span class="file-control v-from " href="javascript:;" style="height:30px"/>')).parent()
                        .append($('<div class="file-container" style="cursor: pointer"/>')
                        .append('<span class="file-text">Chưa có file được chọn</span>')
                        .append('<span class="file-button btn-chose-file" style="width:70px">Chọn file</span>'))
                        .append('<span class="btn-delete-file glyphicons glyphicons-minus-sign" title="Xóa file"></span>')
                        .find('input[type="file"]').trigger('change');
    };

    $.fn.removeMandatoryNote = function() {
        return $(this).parent().prev().filter('label').find('font[color="red"]').remove();
    }
    $.fn.inputReplaceTitle2PlaceHolder = function() {
        $(this).each(function(i, el) {
            if($(el).attr('title')) {
                $(el).attr("placeholder", $(el).attr('title'));
            }
        })
    }
})
</script>

<script>

	$(function(){
		$('.container-page').css("left", "100px");
		$('.container-page').css("margin-right", "80px");
		
		$('#toggleMenubar').on('click', function(){
			var className = $('#sidebar').attr('class');
			if(className === 'active'){
				$('.container-page').css("left", "100px");
				$('.container-page').css("margin-right", "80px");
                window.dispatchEvent(new Event('resize'));
			}
			else{
				$('.container-page').css("left", "240px");
				$('.container-page').css("margin-right", "220px");
                window.dispatchEvent(new Event('resize'));
			}
		});
	});
</script>

<script>

    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('.select2').select2();
    });

    $(document).ready(function () {
        initChosen();
        // đưa select xuống dưới để error hiển thị phía dưới
        setTimeout(function () {
            $('select').each(function (i, el) {
                $(el).next().append($(el));
            })
        }, 100);
    });

    document.getElementById('formSearch').onkeydown = function (event){
        if (event.which == 13 || event.keyCode == 13) {
            processSearchGroup()
        }
    }

    $('#groupName').on('keypress', function (event) {
        if (event.which == 13 || event.keyCode == 13) {
            processSearchGroup()
        } else {
            var regex = new RegExp("^[.a-zA-Z0-9aAàÀảẢãÃáÁạẠăĂằẰẳẲẵẴắẮặẶâÂầẦẩẨẫẪấẤậẬbBcCdDđĐeEèÈẻẺẽẼéÉẹẸêÊềỀểỂễỄếẾệỆ fFgGhHiIìÌỉỈĩĨíÍịỊjJkKlLmMnNoOòÒỏỎõÕóÓọỌôÔồỒổỔỗỖốỐộỘơƠờỜởỞỡỠớỚợỢpPqQrRsStTu UùÙủỦũŨúÚụỤưƯừỪửỬữỮứỨựỰvVwWxXyYỳỲỷỶỹỸýÝỵỴzZ]+$");
            var key = String.fromCharCode(!event.charCode ? event.which : event.charCode);
            if (!regex.test(key)) {
                document.getElementById('checkGroupName').style.display = 'block';
                setTimeout(function (){document.getElementById('checkGroupName').style.display = 'none';}, 4000)
                event.preventDefault();
                return false;
            } else {
                document.getElementById('checkGroupName').style.display = 'none';
            }
        }
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        $(".select2-multiple").select2({
            theme: "bootstrap",
            placeholder: "---------- Chọn ----------" ,
            containerCssClass: ':all:',
            multiple: true,
        });
    });

    $(function () {
        $('#groupModal').modal('show');
    });
    $(document).ready(function () {
        initChosen();
        // đưa select xuống dưới để error hiển thị phía dưới
        setTimeout(function () {
            $('select').each(function (i, el) {
                $(el).next().append($(el));
            })
        }, 100);
    });

    function loadCategoriesSave(value) {
        document.getElementById('checkResultEn').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('checkResult').style.display = 'none';
        $('#categoryId').removeAttr("disabled");
        $('#categoryId').empty();
        $('#categoryId').val(null).trigger('change');
        jQuery.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: /VRS/ +'api/v1/categories/edit?categoryType=' + value,
            success: function (res) {
                var items = '';
                $.each(res.data, function (i, obj) {
                    items += "<option value='" + obj.categoryId + "'>" + obj.name + "</option>";
                });
                $('#categoryId').html(items);
            }
        })
    }
    function clearWarning() {
        document.getElementById('checkResultEn').style.display = 'none';
        document.getElementById('checkResult').style.display = 'none';
    }
    $('#name').on('keypress', function (event) {
        if (event.which != 13 || event.keyCode != 13) {
            var regex = new RegExp("^[.a-zA-Z0-9aAàÀảẢãÃáÁạẠăĂằẰẳẲẵẴắẮặẶâÂầẦẩẨẫẪấẤậẬbBcCdDđĐeEèÈẻẺẽẼéÉẹẸêÊềỀểỂễỄếẾệỆ fFgGhHiIìÌỉỈĩĨíÍịỊjJkKlLmMnNoOòÒỏỎõÕóÓọỌôÔồỒổỔỗỖốỐộỘơƠờỜởỞỡỠớỚợỢpPqQrRsStTu UùÙủỦũŨúÚụỤưƯừỪửỬữỮứỨựỰvVwWxXyYỳỲỷỶỹỸýÝỵỴzZ]+$");
            var key = String.fromCharCode(!event.charCode ? event.which : event.charCode);
            if (!regex.test(key)) {
                document.getElementById('checkResult').style.display = 'block';
                event.preventDefault();
                return false;
            } else {
                document.getElementById('checkResult').style.display = 'none';
            }
        }
    });

    $('#nameEn').on('keypress', function (event) {
        if (event.which != 13 || event.keyCode != 13) {
            var regex = new RegExp("^[.a-zA-Z0-9aAàÀảẢãÃáÁạẠăĂằẰẳẲẵẴắẮặẶâÂầẦẩẨẫẪấẤậẬbBcCdDđĐeEèÈẻẺẽẼéÉẹẸêÊềỀểỂễỄếẾệỆ fFgGhHiIìÌỉỈĩĨíÍịỊjJkKlLmMnNoOòÒỏỎõÕóÓọỌôÔồỒổỔỗỖốỐộỘơƠờỜởỞỡỠớỚợỢpPqQrRsStTu UùÙủỦũŨúÚụỤưƯừỪửỬữỮứỨựỰvVwWxXyYỳỲỷỶỹỸýÝỵỴzZ]+$");
            var key = String.fromCharCode(!event.charCode ? event.which : event.charCode);
            if (!regex.test(key)) {
                document.getElementById('checkResultEn').style.display = 'block';
                event.preventDefault();
                return false;
            } else {
                document.getElementById('checkResultEn').style.display = 'none';
            }
        }
    });

    $('#nameEn').click(function (){
        document.getElementById('checkResult').style.display = 'none';
    });

    $('#name').click(function (){
        document.getElementById('checkResultEn').style.display = 'none';
    });
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    /* Tìm kiếm */
    function processSearchGroup() {
        if ($('#groupFormSearch').validationEngine('validate')) {
            var areaId = "searchResult";
            var actionUrl = "/VRS/groups/search?";
            $("#groupFormSearch").val($("#groupFormSearch").val().trim());
            var category = $('#category').val();
            var formData = $('#groupFormSearch').serializeArray();
            if (Array.isArray(formData)) {
                formData.push({"name": "category", "value": category});
            }
            dttUpdateAjaxCheckToken("GET", areaId, actionUrl, formData, null, 'Token hết hạn');
        }
    }

    $(function () {
        processSearchGroup();
    });

    function openGroupModal() {
        var areaId = "groupModal";
        var actionUrl = "/VRS/groups/add";
        var formData = "";
        dttUpdateAjaxCheckToken("GET", areaId, actionUrl, formData, null, 'Token hết hạn');
    }

    function openEditGroupModal(id) {
        var areaId = "groupEditModal";
        var actionUrl = "/VRS/groups/" + id + "/edit";
        var formData = "";
        dttUpdateAjaxCheckToken("GET", areaId, actionUrl, formData, null, 'Token hết hạn');
    }

    function processDeleteGroup(id) {
        var message = 'Bạn có muốn xóa bản ghi hiện tại?';
        if (id && dttConfirmDelete(message)) {
            var areaId = "saveResultDisplayTag";
            var actionUrl = "/VRS/groups/delete/" + id;
            dttDeferredAjaxCheckToken("POST", areaId, actionUrl, "", "", 'Token hết hạn').done(function () {
                callbackAfterSaveGroup();
            });
        }
    }

    function processSaveGroup() {
        var message = 'Bạn có muốn lưu lại thông tin?';
        var lst = $('#categoryId').val();
        var valid = $('#catGroupForm').validationEngine('validate')
        if (lst == null || lst == undefined || lst.length < 2) {
            document.getElementById('checkCategory').style.display = 'block';
        } else {
            document.getElementById('checkCategory').style.display = 'none';
            if (valid && dttConfirmSave(message)) {
                var areaId = "saveResultDisplayTag";
                var actionUrl = "/VRS/groups/add";

                var formData = $('#catGroupForm').serializeArray();
                if (Array.isArray(formData)) {
                    formData.push({"name": "categoryId", "value": lst});
                }
                dttUpdateAjaxCheckToken("POST", areaId, actionUrl, formData, null, 'Token hết hạn');
            }
        }
    }

    function processEditGroup(id) {
        var message = 'Bạn có muốn lưu lại thông tin?';
        var lst = $('#categoryEditId').val();
        var valid = $('#catGroupEditForm').validationEngine('validate')
        if (lst == null || lst == undefined || lst.length < 2) {
            document.getElementById('checkCategoryEdit').style.display = 'block';
        } else {
            document.getElementById('checkCategoryEdit').style.display = 'none';
            if (valid && dttConfirmSave(message)) {
                var areaId = "saveResultDisplayTag";
                var actionUrl = "/VRS/groups/" + id + "/edit";
                var formData = $('#catGroupEditForm').serializeArray();
                if (Array.isArray(formData)) {
                    formData.push({"name": "categoryId", "value": lst});
                }
                dttUpdateAjaxCheckToken("POST", areaId, actionUrl, formData, null, 'Token hết hạn');
            }
        }
    }

    function callbackAfterSaveGroup() {
        $('#groupModal').modal('hide');
        processSearchGroup();
        scrollTop();
    }

    function callbackAfterUpdateGroup() {
        $('#groupEditModal').modal('hide');
        processSearchGroup();
        scrollTop();
    }

    function loadCategories(value) {
        $('#category').empty()
        $('#category').val(null).trigger('change');
        jQuery.ajax({
            type: 'GET',
            url: /VRS/ +'api/v1/categories?categoryType=' + value,
            success: function (res) {
                var items = "<option value=''>---------Tất cả---------</option>";
                $.each(res.data, function (i, obj) {
                    items += "<option value='" + obj.categoryId + "'>" + obj.name + "</option>";
                });
                $('#category').html(items);
                $('#category').val("").trigger('change');
            },
            error: function (e) {
                console.log('erros', e);
            }
        })
    }

    function showTags(id) {
        $('.show-more-' + id).toggle();
        $('.hide-tags-' + id).toggle();
    }

</script>
		</div>
    </div>
